sched.NextPod(logger)\n    69→\tif err != nil {\n    70→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error while retrieving next pod from scheduling queue\")\n    71→\t\treturn\n    72→\t}\n    73→\t// pod could be nil when schedulerQueue is closed\n    74→\tif podInfo == nil || podInfo.Pod == nil {\n    75→\t\treturn\n    76→\t}\n    77→\n    78→\tpod := podInfo.Pod\n    79→\t// TODO(knelasevero): Remove duplicated keys from log entry calls\n    80→\t// When contextualized logging hits GA\n    81→\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/111672\n    82→\tlogger = klog.LoggerWithValues(logger, \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n    83→\tctx = klog.NewContext(ctx, logger)\n    84→\tlogger.V(4).Info(\"About to try and schedule pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n    85→\n    86→\tfwk, err := sched.frameworkForPod(pod)\n    87→\tif err != nil {\n    88→\t\t// This shouldn't happen, because we only accept for scheduling the pods\n    89→\t\t// which specify a scheduler name that matches one of the profiles.\n    90→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error occurred\")\n    91→\t\treturn\n    92→\t}\n    93→\tif sched.skipPodSchedule(ctx, fwk, pod) {\n    94→\t\treturn\n    95→\t}\n    96→\n    97→\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"Attempting to schedule pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n    98→\n    99→\t// Synchronously attempt to find a fit for the pod.\n   100→\tstart := time.Now()\n   101→\tstate := framework.NewCycleState()\n   102→\tstate.SetRecordPluginMetrics(rand.Intn(100) < pluginMetricsSamplePercent)\n   103→\n   104→\t// Initialize an empty podsToActivate struct, which will be filled up by plugins or stay empty.\n   105→\tpodsToActivate := framework.NewPodsToActivate()\n   106→\tstate.Write(framework.PodsToActivateKey, podsToActivate)\n   107→\n   108→\tschedulingCycleCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n   109→\tdefer cancel()\n   110→\n   111→\tscheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, status := sched.schedulingCycle(schedulingCycleCtx, state, fwk, podInfo, start, podsToActivate)\n   112→\tif !status.IsSuccess() {\n   113→\t\tsched.FailureHandler(schedulingCycleCtx, fwk, assumedPodInfo, status, scheduleResult.nominatingInfo, start)\n   114→\t\treturn\n   115→\t}\n   116→\n   117→\t// bind the pod to its host asynchronously (we can do this b/c of the assumption step above).\n   118→\tgo func() {\n   119→\t\tbindingCycleCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n   120→\t\tdefer cancel()\n   121→\n   122→\t\tmetrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.Binding).Inc()\n   123→\t\tdefer metrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.Binding).Dec()\n   124→\n   125→\t\tstatus := sched.bindingCycle(bindingCycleCtx, state, fwk, scheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, start, podsToActivate)\n   126→\t\tif !status.IsSuccess() {\n   127→\t\t\tsched.handleBindingCycleError(bindingCycleCtx, state, fwk, assumedPodInfo, start, scheduleResult, status)\n   128→\t\t\treturn\n   129→\t\t}\n   130→\t\t// Usually, DonePod is called inside the scheduling queue,\n   131→\t\t// but in this case, we need to call it here because this Pod won't go back to the scheduling queue.\n   132→\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Done(assumedPodInfo.Pod.UID)\n   133→\t}()\n   134→}\n   135→\n   136→var clearNominatedNode = &framework.NominatingInfo{NominatingMode: framework.ModeOverride, NominatedNodeName: \"\"}\n   137→\n   138→// schedulingCycle tries to schedule a single Pod.\n   139→func (sched *Scheduler) schedulingCycle(\n   140→\tctx context.Context,\n   141→\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   142→\tfwk framework.Framework,\n   143→\tpodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n   144→\tstart time.Time,\n   145→\tpodsToActivate *framework.PodsToActivate,\n   146→) (ScheduleResult, *framework.QueuedPodInfo, *framework.Status) {\n   147→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   148→\tpod := podInfo.Pod\n   149→\tscheduleResult, err := sched.SchedulePod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n   150→\tif err != nil {\n   151→\t\tdefer func() {\n   152→\t\t\tmetrics.SchedulingAlgorithmLatency.Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n   153→\t\t}()\n   154→\t\tif err == ErrNoNodesAvailable {\n   155→\t\t\tstatus := framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable).WithError(err)\n   156→\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, status\n   157→\t\t}\n   158→\n   159→\t\tfitError, ok := err.(*framework.FitError)\n   160→\t\tif !ok {\n   161→\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Error selecting node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n   162→\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, podInfo, framework.AsStatus(err)\n   163→\t\t}\n   164→\n   165→\t\t// SchedulePod() may have failed because the pod would not fit on any host, so we try to\n   166→\t\t// preempt, with the expectation that the next time the pod is tried for scheduling it\n   167→\t\t// will fit due to the preemption. It is also possible that a different pod will schedule\n   168→\t\t// into the resources that were preempted, but this is harmless.\n   169→\n   170→\t\tif !fwk.HasPostFilterPlugins() {\n   171→\t\t\tlogger.V(3).Info(\"No PostFilter plugins are registered, so no preemption will be performed\")\n   172→\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{}, podInfo, framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n   173→\t\t}\n   174→\n   175→\t\t// Run PostFilter plugins to attempt to make the pod schedulable in a future scheduling cycle.\n   176→\t\tresult, status := fwk.RunPostFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod, fitError.Diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n   177→\t\tmsg := status.Message()\n   178→\t\tfitError.Diagnosis.PostFilterMsg = msg\n   179→\t\tif status.Code() == framework.Error {\n   180→\t\t\tlogger.Error(nil, \"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n   181→\t\t} else {\n   182→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PostFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n   183→\t\t}\n   184→\n   185→\t\tvar nominatingInfo *framework.NominatingInfo\n   186→\t\tif result != nil {\n   187→\t\t\tnominatingInfo = result.NominatingInfo\n   188→\t\t}\n   189→\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: nominatingInfo}, podInfo, framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable).WithError(err)\n   190→\t}\n   191→\n   192→\tmetrics.SchedulingAlgorithmLatency.Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n   193→\t// Tell the cache to assume that a pod now is running on a given node, even though it hasn't been bound yet.\n   194→\t// This allows us to keep scheduling without waiting on binding to occur.\n   195→\tassumedPodInfo := podInfo.DeepCopy()\n   196→\tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n   197→\t// assume modifies `assumedPod` by setting NodeName=scheduleResult.SuggestedHost\n   198→\terr = sched.assume(logger, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n   199→\tif err != nil {\n   200→\t\t// This is most probably result of a BUG in retrying logic.\n   201→\t\t// We report an error here so that pod scheduling can be retried.\n   202→\t\t// This relies on the fact that Error will check if the pod has been bound\n   203→\t\t// to a node and if so will not add it back to the unscheduled pods queue\n   204→\t\t// (otherwise this would cause an infinite loop).\n   205→\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.AsStatus(err)\n   206→\t}\n   207→\n   208→\t// Run the Reserve method of reserve plugins.\n   209→\tif sts := fwk.RunReservePluginsReserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !sts.IsSuccess() {\n   210→\t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n   211→\t\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n   212→\t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n   213→\t\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n   214→\t\t}\n   215→\n   216→\t\tif sts.IsRejected() {\n   217→\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n   218→\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n   219→\t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n   220→\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n   221→\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap: framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: sts},\n   222→\t\t\t\t},\n   223→\t\t\t}\n   224→\t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(sts)\n   225→\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.NewStatus(sts.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n   226→\t\t}\n   227→\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, sts\n   228→\t}\n   229→\n   230→\t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n   231→\trunPermitStatus := fwk.RunPermitPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n   232→\tif !runPermitStatus.IsWait() && !runPermitStatus.IsSuccess() {\n   233→\t\t// trigger un-reserve to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n   234→\t\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n   235→\t\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n   236→\t\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"Scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n   237→\t\t}\n   238→\n   239→\t\tif runPermitStatus.IsRejected() {\n   240→\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n   241→\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n   242→\t\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n   243→\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n   244→\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap: framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: runPermitStatus},\n   245→\t\t\t\t},\n   246→\t\t\t}\n   247→\t\t\tfitErr.Diagnosis.AddPluginStatus(runPermitStatus)\n   248→\t\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, framework.NewStatus(runPermitStatus.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n   249→\t\t}\n   250→\n   251→\t\treturn ScheduleResult{nominatingInfo: clearNominatedNode}, assumedPodInfo, runPermitStatus\n   252→\t}\n   253→\n   254→\t// At the end of a successful scheduling cycle, pop and move up Pods if needed.\n   255→\tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n   256→\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n   257→\t\t// Clear the entries after activation.\n   258→\t\tpodsToActivate.Map = make(map[string]*v1.Pod)\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\treturn scheduleResult, assumedPodInfo, nil\n   262→}\n   263→\n   264→// bindingCycle tries to bind an assumed Pod.\n   265→func (sched *Scheduler) bindingCycle(\n   266→\tctx context.Context,\n   267→\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   268→\tfwk framework.Framework,\n   269→\tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n   270→\tassumedPodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n   271→\tstart time.Time,\n   272→\tpodsToActivate *framework.PodsToActivate) *framework.Status {\n   273→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   274→\n   275→\tassumedPod := assumedPodInfo.Pod\n   276→\n   277→\t// Run \"permit\" plugins.\n   278→\tif status := fwk.WaitOnPermit(ctx, assumedPod); !status.IsSuccess() {\n   279→\t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n   280→\t\t\tfitErr := &framework.FitError{\n   281→\t\t\t\tNumAllNodes: 1,\n   282→\t\t\t\tPod:         assumedPodInfo.Pod,\n   283→\t\t\t\tDiagnosis: framework.Diagnosis{\n   284→\t\t\t\t\tNodeToStatusMap:      framework.NodeToStatusMap{scheduleResult.SuggestedHost: status},\n   285→\t\t\t\t\tUnschedulablePlugins: sets.New(status.Plugin()),\n   286→\t\t\t\t},\n   287→\t\t\t}\n   288→\t\t\treturn framework.NewStatus(status.Code()).WithError(fitErr)\n   289→\t\t}\n   290→\t\treturn status\n   291→\t}\n   292→\n   293→\t// Run \"prebind\" plugins.\n   294→\tif status := fwk.RunPreBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost); !status.IsSuccess() {\n   295→\t\treturn status\n   296→\t}\n   297→\n   298→\t// Run \"bind\" plugins.\n   299→\tif status := sched.bind(ctx, fwk, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, state); !status.IsSuccess() {\n   300→\t\treturn status\n   301→\t}\n   302→\n   303→\t// Calculating nodeResourceString can be heavy. Avoid it if klog verbosity is below 2.\n   304→\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Successfully bound pod to node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(assumedPod), \"node\", scheduleResult.SuggestedHost, \"evaluatedNodes\", scheduleResult.EvaluatedNodes, \"feasibleNodes\", scheduleResult.FeasibleNodes)\n   305→\tmetrics.PodScheduled(fwk.ProfileName(), metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n   306→\tmetrics.PodSchedulingAttempts.Observe(float64(assumedPodInfo.Attempts))\n   307→\tif assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp != nil {\n   308→\t\tmetrics.PodSchedulingDuration.WithLabelValues(getAttemptsLabel(assumedPodInfo)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(*assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp))\n   309→\t\tmetrics.PodSchedulingSLIDuration.WithLabelValues(getAttemptsLabel(assumedPodInfo)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(*assumedPodInfo.InitialAttemptTimestamp))\n   310→\t}\n   311→\t// Run \"postbind\" plugins.\n   312→\tfwk.RunPostBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n   313→\n   314→\t// At the end of a successful binding cycle, move up Pods if needed.\n   315→\tif len(podsToActivate.Map) != 0 {\n   316→\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Activate(logger, podsToActivate.Map)\n   317→\t\t// Unlike the logic in schedulingCycle(), we don't bother deleting the entries\n   318→\t\t// as `podsToActivate.Map` is no longer consumed.\n   319→\t}\n   320→\n   321→\treturn nil\n   322→}\n   323→\n   324→func (sched *Scheduler) handleBindingCycleError(\n   325→\tctx context.Context,\n   326→\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   327→\tfwk framework.Framework,\n   328→\tpodInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo,\n   329→\tstart time.Time,\n   330→\tscheduleResult ScheduleResult,\n   331→\tstatus *framework.Status) {\n   332→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   333→\n   334→\tassumedPod := podInfo.Pod\n   335→\t// trigger un-reserve plugins to clean up state associated with the reserved Pod\n   336→\tfwk.RunReservePluginsUnreserve(ctx, state, assumedPod, scheduleResult.SuggestedHost)\n   337→\tif forgetErr := sched.Cache.ForgetPod(logger, assumedPod); forgetErr != nil {\n   338→\t\tlogger.Error(forgetErr, \"scheduler cache ForgetPod failed\")\n   339→\t} else {\n   340→\t\t// \"Forget\"ing an assumed Pod in binding cycle should be treated as a PodDelete event,\n   341→\t\t// as the assumed Pod had occupied a certain amount of resources in scheduler cache.\n   342→\t\t//\n   343→\t\t// Avoid moving the assumed Pod itself as it's always Unschedulable.\n   344→\t\t// It's intentional to \"defer\" this operation; otherwise MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue() would\n   345→\t\t// add this event to in-flight events and thus move the assumed pod to backoffQ anyways if the plugins don't have appropriate QueueingHint.\n   346→\t\tif status.IsRejected() {\n   347→\t\t\tdefer sched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, internalqueue.AssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, func(pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n   348→\t\t\t\treturn assumedPod.UID != pod.UID\n   349→\t\t\t})\n   350→\t\t} else {\n   351→\t\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.MoveAllToActiveOrBackoffQueue(logger, internalqueue.AssignedPodDelete, assumedPod, nil, nil)\n   352→\t\t}\n   353→\t}\n   354→\n   355→\tsched.FailureHandler(ctx, fwk, podInfo, status, clearNominatedNode, start)\n   356→}\n   357→\n   358→func (sched *Scheduler) frameworkForPod(pod *v1.Pod) (framework.Framework, error) {\n   359→\tfwk, ok := sched.Profiles[pod.Spec.SchedulerName]\n   360→\tif !ok {\n   361→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"profile not found for scheduler name %q\", pod.Spec.SchedulerName)\n   362→\t}\n   363→\treturn fwk, nil\n   364→}\n   365→\n   366→// skipPodSchedule returns true if we could skip scheduling the pod for specified cases.\n   367→func (sched *Scheduler) skipPodSchedule(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n   368→\t// Case 1: pod is being deleted.\n   369→\tif pod.DeletionTimestamp != nil {\n   370→\t\tfwk.EventRecorder().Eventf(pod, nil, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"FailedScheduling\", \"Scheduling\", \"skip schedule deleting pod: %v/%v\", pod.Namespace, pod.Name)\n   371→\t\tklog.FromContext(ctx).V(3).Info(\"Skip schedule deleting pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n   372→\t\treturn true\n   373→\t}\n   374→\n   375→\t// Case 2: pod that has been assumed could be skipped.\n   376→\t// An assumed pod can be added again to the scheduling queue if it got an update event\n   377→\t// during its previous scheduling cycle but before getting assumed.\n   378→\tisAssumed, err := sched.Cache.IsAssumedPod(pod)\n   379→\tif err != nil {\n   380→\t\t// TODO(91633): pass ctx into a revised HandleError\n   381→\t\tutilruntime.HandleError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to check whether pod %s/%s is assumed: %v\", pod.Namespace, pod.Name, err))\n   382→\t\treturn false\n   383→\t}\n   384→\treturn isAssumed\n   385→}\n   386→\n   387→// schedulePod tries to schedule the given pod to one of the nodes in the node list.\n   388→// If it succeeds, it will return the name of the node.\n   389→// If it fails, it will return a FitError with reasons.\n   390→func (sched *Scheduler) schedulePod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) (result ScheduleResult, err error) {\n   391→\ttrace := utiltrace.New(\"Scheduling\", utiltrace.Field{Key: \"namespace\", Value: pod.Namespace}, utiltrace.Field{Key: \"name\", Value: pod.Name})\n   392→\tdefer trace.LogIfLong(100 * time.Millisecond)\n   393→\tif err := sched.Cache.UpdateSnapshot(klog.FromContext(ctx), sched.nodeInfoSnapshot); err != nil {\n   394→\t\treturn result, err\n   395→\t}\n   396→\ttrace.Step(\"Snapshotting scheduler cache and node infos done\")\n   397→\n   398→\tif sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes() == 0 {\n   399→\t\treturn result, ErrNoNodesAvailable\n   400→\t}\n   401→\n   402→\tfeasibleNodes, diagnosis, err := sched.findNodesThatFitPod(ctx, fwk, state, pod)\n   403→\tif err != nil {\n   404→\t\treturn result, err\n   405→\t}\n   406→\ttrace.Step(\"Computing predicates done\")\n   407→\n   408→\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n   409→\t\treturn result, &framework.FitError{\n   410→\t\t\tPod:         pod,\n   411→\t\t\tNumAllNodes: sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NumNodes(),\n   412→\t\t\tDiagnosis:   diagnosis,\n   413→\t\t}\n   414→\t}\n   415→\n   416→\t// When only one node after predicate, just use it.\n   417→\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 1 {\n   418→\t\treturn ScheduleResult{\n   419→\t\t\tSuggestedHost:  feasibleNodes[0].Node().Name,\n   420→\t\t\tEvaluatedNodes: 1 + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n   421→\t\t\tFeasibleNodes:  1,\n   422→\t\t}, nil\n   423→\t}\n   424→\n   425→\tpriorityList, err := prioritizeNodes(ctx, sched.Extenders, fwk, state, pod, feasibleNodes)\n   426→\tif err != nil {\n   427→\t\treturn result, err\n   428→\t}\n   429→\n   430→\thost, _, err := selectHost(priorityList, numberOfHighestScoredNodesToReport)\n   431→\ttrace.Step(\"Prioritizing done\")\n   432→\n   433→\treturn ScheduleResult{\n   434→\t\tSuggestedHost:  host,\n   435→\t\tEvaluatedNodes: len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap),\n   436→\t\tFeasibleNodes:  len(feasibleNodes),\n   437→\t}, err\n   438→}\n   439→\n   440→// Filters the nodes to find the ones that fit the pod based on the framework\n   441→// filter plugins and filter extenders.\n   442→func (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatFitPod(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, pod *v1.Pod) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, framework.Diagnosis, error) {\n   443→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   444→\tdiagnosis := framework.Diagnosis{\n   445→\t\tNodeToStatusMap: make(framework.NodeToStatusMap),\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\tallNodes, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.NodeInfos().List()\n   449→\tif err != nil {\n   450→\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n   451→\t}\n   452→\t// Run \"prefilter\" plugins.\n   453→\tpreRes, s := fwk.RunPreFilterPlugins(ctx, state, pod)\n   454→\tif !s.IsSuccess() {\n   455→\t\tif !s.IsRejected() {\n   456→\t\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, s.AsError()\n   457→\t\t}\n   458→\t\t// All nodes in NodeToStatusMap will have the same status so that they can be handled in the preemption.\n   459→\t\t// Some non trivial refactoring is needed to avoid this copy.\n   460→\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n   461→\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = s\n   462→\t\t}\n   463→\n   464→\t\t// Record the messages from PreFilter in Diagnosis.PreFilterMsg.\n   465→\t\tmsg := s.Message()\n   466→\t\tdiagnosis.PreFilterMsg = msg\n   467→\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Status after running PreFilter plugins for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"status\", msg)\n   468→\t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(s)\n   469→\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, nil\n   470→\t}\n   471→\n   472→\t// \"NominatedNodeName\" can potentially be set in a previous scheduling cycle as a result of preemption.\n   473→\t// This node is likely the only candidate that will fit the pod, and hence we try it first before iterating over all nodes.\n   474→\tif len(pod.Status.NominatedNodeName) > 0 {\n   475→\t\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.evaluateNominatedNode(ctx, pod, fwk, state, diagnosis)\n   476→\t\tif err != nil {\n   477→\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Evaluation failed on nominated node\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"node\", pod.Status.NominatedNodeName)\n   478→\t\t}\n   479→\t\t// Nominated node passes all the filters, scheduler is good to assign this node to the pod.\n   480→\t\tif len(feasibleNodes) != 0 {\n   481→\t\t\treturn feasibleNodes, diagnosis, nil\n   482→\t\t}\n   483→\t}\n   484→\n   485→\tnodes := allNodes\n   486→\tif !preRes.AllNodes() {\n   487→\t\tnodes = make([]*framework.NodeInfo, 0, len(preRes.NodeNames))\n   488→\t\tfor _, n := range allNodes {\n   489→\t\t\tif !preRes.NodeNames.Has(n.Node().Name) {\n   490→\t\t\t\t// We consider Nodes that are filtered out by PreFilterResult as rejected via UnschedulableAndUnresolvable.\n   491→\t\t\t\t// We have to record them in NodeToStatusMap so that they won't be considered as candidates in the preemption.\n   492→\t\t\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[n.Node().Name] = framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, \"node is filtered out by the prefilter result\")\n   493→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   494→\t\t\t}\n   495→\t\t\tnodes = append(nodes, n)\n   496→\t\t}\n   497→\t}\n   498→\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, nodes)\n   499→\t// always try to update the sched.nextStartNodeIndex regardless of whether an error has occurred\n   500→\t// this is helpful to make sure that all the nodes have a chance to be searched\n   501→\tprocessedNodes := len(feasibleNodes) + len(diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n   502→\tsched.nextStartNodeIndex = (sched.nextStartNodeIndex + processedNodes) % len(nodes)\n   503→\tif err != nil {\n   504→\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n   505→\t}\n   506→\n   507→\tfeasibleNodesAfterExtender, err := findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n   508→\tif err != nil {\n   509→\t\treturn nil, diagnosis, err\n   510→\t}\n   511→\tif len(feasibleNodesAfterExtender) != len(feasibleNodes) {\n   512→\t\t// Extenders filtered out some nodes.\n   513→\t\t//\n   514→\t\t// Extender doesn't support any kind of requeueing feature like EnqueueExtensions in the scheduling framework.\n   515→\t\t// When Extenders reject some Nodes and the pod ends up being unschedulable,\n   516→\t\t// we put framework.ExtenderName to pInfo.UnschedulablePlugins.\n   517→\t\t// This Pod will be requeued from unschedulable pod pool to activeQ/backoffQ\n   518→\t\t// by any kind of cluster events.\n   519→\t\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/122019\n   520→\t\tif diagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins == nil {\n   521→\t\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins = sets.New[string]()\n   522→\t\t}\n   523→\t\tdiagnosis.UnschedulablePlugins.Insert(framework.ExtenderName)\n   524→\t}\n   525→\n   526→\treturn feasibleNodesAfterExtender, diagnosis, nil\n   527→}\n   528→\n   529→func (sched *Scheduler) evaluateNominatedNode(ctx context.Context, pod *v1.Pod, fwk framework.Framework, state *framework.CycleState, diagnosis framework.Diagnosis) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n   530→\tnnn := pod.Status.NominatedNodeName\n   531→\tnodeInfo, err := sched.nodeInfoSnapshot.Get(nnn)\n   532→\tif err != nil {\n   533→\t\treturn nil, err\n   534→\t}\n   535→\tnode := []*framework.NodeInfo{nodeInfo}\n   536→\tfeasibleNodes, err := sched.findNodesThatPassFilters(ctx, fwk, state, pod, &diagnosis, node)\n   537→\tif err != nil {\n   538→\t\treturn nil, err\n   539→\t}\n   540→\n   541→\tfeasibleNodes, err = findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx, sched.Extenders, pod, feasibleNodes, diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap)\n   542→\tif err != nil {\n   543→\t\treturn nil, err\n   544→\t}\n   545→\n   546→\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   547→}\n   548→\n   549→// hasScoring checks if scoring nodes is configured.\n   550→func (sched *Scheduler) hasScoring(fwk framework.Framework) bool {\n   551→\tif fwk.HasScorePlugins() {\n   552→\t\treturn true\n   553→\t}\n   554→\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n   555→\t\tif extender.IsPrioritizer() {\n   556→\t\t\treturn true\n   557→\t\t}\n   558→\t}\n   559→\treturn false\n   560→}\n   561→\n   562→// hasExtenderFilters checks if any extenders filter nodes.\n   563→func (sched *Scheduler) hasExtenderFilters() bool {\n   564→\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n   565→\t\tif extender.IsFilter() {\n   566→\t\t\treturn true\n   567→\t\t}\n   568→\t}\n   569→\treturn false\n   570→}\n   571→\n   572→// findNodesThatPassFilters finds the nodes that fit the filter plugins.\n   573→func (sched *Scheduler) findNodesThatPassFilters(\n   574→\tctx context.Context,\n   575→\tfwk framework.Framework,\n   576→\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   577→\tpod *v1.Pod,\n   578→\tdiagnosis *framework.Diagnosis,\n   579→\tnodes []*framework.NodeInfo) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n   580→\tnumAllNodes := len(nodes)\n   581→\tnumNodesToFind := sched.numFeasibleNodesToFind(fwk.PercentageOfNodesToScore(), int32(numAllNodes))\n   582→\tif !sched.hasExtenderFilters() && !sched.hasScoring(fwk) {\n   583→\t\tnumNodesToFind = 1\n   584→\t}\n   585→\n   586→\t// Create feasible list with enough space to avoid growing it\n   587→\t// and allow assigning.\n   588→\tfeasibleNodes := make([]*framework.NodeInfo, numNodesToFind)\n   589→\n   590→\tif !fwk.HasFilterPlugins() {\n   591→\t\tfor i := range feasibleNodes {\n   592→\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[i] = nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n   593→\t\t}\n   594→\t\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   595→\t}\n   596→\n   597→\terrCh := parallelize.NewErrorChannel()\n   598→\tvar feasibleNodesLen int32\n   599→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n   600→\tdefer cancel()\n   601→\n   602→\ttype nodeStatus struct {\n   603→\t\tnode   string\n   604→\t\tstatus *framework.Status\n   605→\t}\n   606→\tresult := make([]*nodeStatus, numAllNodes)\n   607→\tcheckNode := func(i int) {\n   608→\t\t// We check the nodes starting from where we left off in the previous scheduling cycle,\n   609→\t\t// this is to make sure all nodes have the same chance of being examined across pods.\n   610→\t\tnodeInfo := nodes[(sched.nextStartNodeIndex+i)%numAllNodes]\n   611→\t\tstatus := fwk.RunFilterPluginsWithNominatedPods(ctx, state, pod, nodeInfo)\n   612→\t\tif status.Code() == framework.Error {\n   613→\t\t\terrCh.SendErrorWithCancel(status.AsError(), cancel)\n   614→\t\t\treturn\n   615→\t\t}\n   616→\t\tif status.IsSuccess() {\n   617→\t\t\tlength := atomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, 1)\n   618→\t\t\tif length > numNodesToFind {\n   619→\t\t\t\tcancel()\n   620→\t\t\t\tatomic.AddInt32(&feasibleNodesLen, -1)\n   621→\t\t\t} else {\n   622→\t\t\t\tfeasibleNodes[length-1] = nodeInfo\n   623→\t\t\t}\n   624→\t\t} else {\n   625→\t\t\tresult[i] = &nodeStatus{node: nodeInfo.Node().Name, status: status}\n   626→\t\t}\n   627→\t}\n   628→\n   629→\tbeginCheckNode := time.Now()\n   630→\tstatusCode := framework.Success\n   631→\tdefer func() {\n   632→\t\t// We record Filter extension point latency here instead of in framework.go because framework.RunFilterPlugins\n   633→\t\t// function is called for each node, whereas we want to have an overall latency for all nodes per scheduling cycle.\n   634→\t\t// Note that this latency also includes latency for `addNominatedPods`, which calls framework.RunPreFilterAddPod.\n   635→\t\tmetrics.FrameworkExtensionPointDuration.WithLabelValues(metrics.Filter, statusCode.String(), fwk.ProfileName()).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(beginCheckNode))\n   636→\t}()\n   637→\n   638→\t// Stops searching for more nodes once the configured number of feasible nodes\n   639→\t// are found.\n   640→\tfwk.Parallelizer().Until(ctx, numAllNodes, checkNode, metrics.Filter)\n   641→\tfeasibleNodes = feasibleNodes[:feasibleNodesLen]\n   642→\tfor _, item := range result {\n   643→\t\tif item == nil {\n   644→\t\t\tcontinue\n   645→\t\t}\n   646→\t\tdiagnosis.NodeToStatusMap[item.node] = item.status\n   647→\t\tdiagnosis.AddPluginStatus(item.status)\n   648→\t}\n   649→\tif err := errCh.ReceiveError(); err != nil {\n   650→\t\tstatusCode = framework.Error\n   651→\t\treturn feasibleNodes, err\n   652→\t}\n   653→\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   654→}\n   655→\n   656→// numFeasibleNodesToFind returns the number of feasible nodes that once found, the scheduler stops\n   657→// its search for more feasible nodes.\n   658→func (sched *Scheduler) numFeasibleNodesToFind(percentageOfNodesToScore *int32, numAllNodes int32) (numNodes int32) {\n   659→\tif numAllNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\n   660→\t\treturn numAllNodes\n   661→\t}\n   662→\n   663→\t// Use profile percentageOfNodesToScore if it's set. Otherwise, use global percentageOfNodesToScore.\n   664→\tvar percentage int32\n   665→\tif percentageOfNodesToScore != nil {\n   666→\t\tpercentage = *percentageOfNodesToScore\n   667→\t} else {\n   668→\t\tpercentage = sched.percentageOfNodesToScore\n   669→\t}\n   670→\n   671→\tif percentage == 0 {\n   672→\t\tpercentage = int32(50) - numAllNodes/125\n   673→\t\tif percentage < minFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind {\n   674→\t\t\tpercentage = minFeasibleNodesPercentageToFind\n   675→\t\t}\n   676→\t}\n   677→\n   678→\tnumNodes = numAllNodes * percentage / 100\n   679→\tif numNodes < minFeasibleNodesToFind {\n   680→\t\treturn minFeasibleNodesToFind\n   681→\t}\n   682→\n   683→\treturn numNodes\n   684→}\n   685→\n   686→func findNodesThatPassExtenders(ctx context.Context, extenders []framework.Extender, pod *v1.Pod, feasibleNodes []*framework.NodeInfo, statuses framework.NodeToStatusMap) ([]*framework.NodeInfo, error) {\n   687→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   688→\t// Extenders are called sequentially.\n   689→\t// Nodes in original feasibleNodes can be excluded in one extender, and pass on to the next\n   690→\t// extender in a decreasing manner.\n   691→\tfor _, extender := range extenders {\n   692→\t\tif len(feasibleNodes) == 0 {\n   693→\t\t\tbreak\n   694→\t\t}\n   695→\t\tif !extender.IsInterested(pod) {\n   696→\t\t\tcontinue\n   697→\t\t}\n   698→\n   699→\t\t// Status of failed nodes in failedAndUnresolvableMap will be added or overwritten in <statuses>,\n   700→\t\t// so that the scheduler framework can respect the UnschedulableAndUnresolvable status for\n   701→\t\t// particular nodes, and this may eventually improve preemption efficiency.\n   702→\t\t// Note: users are recommended to configure the extenders that may return UnschedulableAndUnresolvable\n   703→\t\t// status ahead of others.\n   704→\t\tfeasibleList, failedMap, failedAndUnresolvableMap, err := extender.Filter(pod, feasibleNodes)\n   705→\t\tif err != nil {\n   706→\t\t\tif extender.IsIgnorable() {\n   707→\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping extender as it returned error and has ignorable flag set\", \"extender\", extender, \"err\", err)\n   708→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   709→\t\t\t}\n   710→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   711→\t\t}\n   712→\n   713→\t\tfor failedNodeName, failedMsg := range failedAndUnresolvableMap {\n   714→\t\t\tvar aggregatedReasons []string\n   715→\t\t\tif _, found := statuses[failedNodeName]; found {\n   716→\t\t\t\taggregatedReasons = statuses[failedNodeName].Reasons()\n   717→\t\t\t}\n   718→\t\t\taggregatedReasons = append(aggregatedReasons, failedMsg)\n   719→\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName] = framework.NewStatus(framework.UnschedulableAndUnresolvable, aggregatedReasons...)\n   720→\t\t}\n   721→\n   722→\t\tfor failedNodeName, failedMsg := range failedMap {\n   723→\t\t\tif _, found := failedAndUnresolvableMap[failedNodeName]; found {\n   724→\t\t\t\t// failedAndUnresolvableMap takes precedence over failedMap\n   725→\t\t\t\t// note that this only happens if the extender returns the node in both maps\n   726→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   727→\t\t\t}\n   728→\t\t\tif _, found := statuses[failedNodeName]; !found {\n   729→\t\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName] = framework.NewStatus(framework.Unschedulable, failedMsg)\n   730→\t\t\t} else {\n   731→\t\t\t\tstatuses[failedNodeName].AppendReason(failedMsg)\n   732→\t\t\t}\n   733→\t\t}\n   734→\n   735→\t\tfeasibleNodes = feasibleList\n   736→\t}\n   737→\treturn feasibleNodes, nil\n   738→}\n   739→\n   740→// prioritizeNodes prioritizes the nodes by running the score plugins,\n   741→// which return a score for each node from the call to RunScorePlugins().\n   742→// The scores from each plugin are added together to make the score for that node, then\n   743→// any extenders are run as well.\n   744→// All scores are finally combined (added) to get the total weighted scores of all nodes\n   745→func prioritizeNodes(\n   746→\tctx context.Context,\n   747→\textenders []framework.Extender,\n   748→\tfwk framework.Framework,\n   749→\tstate *framework.CycleState,\n   750→\tpod *v1.Pod,\n   751→\tnodes []*framework.NodeInfo,\n   752→) ([]framework.NodePluginScores, error) {\n   753→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   754→\t// If no priority configs are provided, then all nodes will have a score of one.\n   755→\t// This is required to generate the priority list in the required format\n   756→\tif len(extenders) == 0 && !fwk.HasScorePlugins() {\n   757→\t\tresult := make([]framework.NodePluginScores, 0, len(nodes))\n   758→\t\tfor i := range nodes {\n   759→\t\t\tresult = append(result, framework.NodePluginScores{\n   760→\t\t\t\tName:       nodes[i].Node().Name,\n   761→\t\t\t\tTotalScore: 1,\n   762→\t\t\t})\n   763→\t\t}\n   764→\t\treturn result, nil\n   765→\t}\n   766→\n   767→\t// Run PreScore plugins.\n   768→\tpreScoreStatus := fwk.RunPreScorePlugins(ctx, state, pod, nodes)\n   769→\tif !preScoreStatus.IsSuccess() {\n   770→\t\treturn nil, preScoreStatus.AsError()\n   771→\t}\n   772→\n   773→\t// Run the Score plugins.\n   774→\tnodesScores, scoreStatus := fwk.RunScorePlugins(ctx, state, pod, nodes)\n   775→\tif !scoreStatus.IsSuccess() {\n   776→\t\treturn nil, scoreStatus.AsError()\n   777→\t}\n   778→\n   779→\t// Additional details logged at level 10 if enabled.\n   780→\tloggerVTen := logger.V(10)\n   781→\tif loggerVTen.Enabled() {\n   782→\t\tfor _, nodeScore := range nodesScores {\n   783→\t\t\tfor _, pluginScore := range nodeScore.Scores {\n   784→\t\t\t\tloggerVTen.Info(\"Plugin scored node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"plugin\", pluginScore.Name, \"node\", nodeScore.Name, \"score\", pluginScore.Score)\n   785→\t\t\t}\n   786→\t\t}\n   787→\t}\n   788→\n   789→\tif len(extenders) != 0 && nodes != nil {\n   790→\t\t// allNodeExtendersScores has all extenders scores for all nodes.\n   791→\t\t// It is keyed with node name.\n   792→\t\tallNodeExtendersScores := make(map[string]*framework.NodePluginScores, len(nodes))\n   793→\t\tvar mu sync.Mutex\n   794→\t\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   795→\t\tfor i := range extenders {\n   796→\t\t\tif !extenders[i].IsInterested(pod) {\n   797→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   798→\t\t\t}\n   799→\t\t\twg.Add(1)\n   800→\t\t\tgo func(extIndex int) {\n   801→\t\t\t\tmetrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.PrioritizingExtender).Inc()\n   802→\t\t\t\tdefer func() {\n   803→\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.Goroutines.WithLabelValues(metrics.PrioritizingExtender).Dec()\n   804→\t\t\t\t\twg.Done()\n   805→\t\t\t\t}()\n   806→\t\t\t\tprioritizedList, weight, err := extenders[extIndex].Prioritize(pod, nodes)\n   807→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   808→\t\t\t\t\t// Prioritization errors from extender can be ignored, let k8s/other extenders determine the priorities\n   809→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Failed to run extender's priority function. No score given by this extender.\", \"error\", err, \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"extender\", extenders[extIndex].Name())\n   810→\t\t\t\t\treturn\n   811→\t\t\t\t}\n   812→\t\t\t\tmu.Lock()\n   813→\t\t\t\tdefer mu.Unlock()\n   814→\t\t\t\tfor i := range *prioritizedList {\n   815→\t\t\t\t\tnodename := (*prioritizedList)[i].Host\n   816→\t\t\t\t\tscore := (*prioritizedList)[i].Score\n   817→\t\t\t\t\tif loggerVTen.Enabled() {\n   818→\t\t\t\t\t\tloggerVTen.Info(\"Extender scored node for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"extender\", extenders[extIndex].Name(), \"node\", nodename, \"score\", score)\n   819→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   820→\n   821→\t\t\t\t\t// MaxExtenderPriority may diverge from the max priority used in the scheduler and defined by MaxNodeScore,\n   822→\t\t\t\t\t// therefore we need to scale the score returned by extenders to the score range used by the scheduler.\n   823→\t\t\t\t\tfinalscore := score * weight * (framework.MaxNodeScore / extenderv1.MaxExtenderPriority)\n   824→\n   825→\t\t\t\t\tif allNodeExtendersScores[nodename] == nil {\n   826→\t\t\t\t\t\tallNodeExtendersScores[nodename] = &framework.NodePluginScores{\n   827→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tName:   nodename,\n   828→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tScores: make([]framework.PluginScore, 0, len(extenders)),\n   829→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   830→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   831→\t\t\t\t\tallNodeExtendersScores[nodename].Scores = append(allNodeExtendersScores[nodename].Scores, framework.PluginScore{\n   832→\t\t\t\t\t\tName:  extenders[extIndex].Name(),\n   833→\t\t\t\t\t\tScore: finalscore,\n   834→\t\t\t\t\t})\n   835→\t\t\t\t\tallNodeExtendersScores[nodename].TotalScore += finalscore\n   836→\t\t\t\t}\n   837→\t\t\t}(i)\n   838→\t\t}\n   839→\t\t// wait for all go routines to finish\n   840→\t\twg.Wait()\n   841→\t\tfor i := range nodesScores {\n   842→\t\t\tif score, ok := allNodeExtendersScores[nodes[i].Node().Name]; ok {\n   843→\t\t\t\tnodesScores[i].Scores = append(nodesScores[i].Scores, score.Scores...)\n   844→\t\t\t\tnodesScores[i].TotalScore += score.TotalScore\n   845→\t\t\t}\n   846→\t\t}\n   847→\t}\n   848→\n   849→\tif loggerVTen.Enabled() {\n   850→\t\tfor i := range nodesScores {\n   851→\t\t\tloggerVTen.Info(\"Calculated node's final score for pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"node\", nodesScores[i].Name, \"score\", nodesScores[i].TotalScore)\n   852→\t\t}\n   853→\t}\n   854→\treturn nodesScores, nil\n   855→}\n   856→\n   857→var errEmptyPriorityList = errors.New(\"empty priorityList\")\n   858→\n   859→// selectHost takes a prioritized list of nodes and then picks one\n   860→// in a reservoir sampling manner from the nodes that had the highest score.\n   861→// It also returns the top {count} Nodes,\n   862→// and the top of the list will be always the selected host.\n   863→func selectHost(nodeScoreList []framework.NodePluginScores, count int) (string, []framework.NodePluginScores, error) {\n   864→\tif len(nodeScoreList) == 0 {\n   865→\t\treturn \"\", nil, errEmptyPriorityList\n   866→\t}\n   867→\n   868→\tvar h nodeScoreHeap = nodeScoreList\n   869→\theap.Init(&h)\n   870→\tcntOfMaxScore := 1\n   871→\tselectedIndex := 0\n   872→\t// The top of the heap is the NodeScoreResult with the highest score.\n   873→\tsortedNodeScoreList := make([]framework.NodePluginScores, 0, count)\n   874→\tsortedNodeScoreList = append(sortedNodeScoreList, heap.Pop(&h).(framework.NodePluginScores))\n   875→\n   876→\t// This for-loop will continue until all Nodes with the highest scores get checked for a reservoir sampling,\n   877→\t// and sortedNodeScoreList gets (count - 1) elements.\n   878→\tfor ns := heap.Pop(&h).(framework.NodePluginScores); ; ns = heap.Pop(&h).(framework.NodePluginScores) {\n   879→\t\tif ns.TotalScore != sortedNodeScoreList[0].TotalScore && len(sortedNodeScoreList) == count {\n   880→\t\t\tbreak\n   881→\t\t}\n   882→\n   883→\t\tif ns.TotalScore == sortedNodeScoreList[0].TotalScore {\n   884→\t\t\tcntOfMaxScore++\n   885→\t\t\tif rand.Intn(cntOfMaxScore) == 0 {\n   886→\t\t\t\t// Replace the candidate with probability of 1/cntOfMaxScore\n   887→\t\t\t\tselectedIndex = cntOfMaxScore - 1\n   888→\t\t\t}\n   889→\t\t}\n   890→\n   891→\t\tsortedNodeScoreList = append(sortedNodeScoreList, ns)\n   892→\n   893→\t\tif h.Len() == 0 {\n   894→\t\t\tbreak\n   895→\t\t}\n   896→\t}\n   897→\n   898→\tif selectedIndex != 0 {\n   899→\t\t// replace the first one with selected one\n   900→\t\tprevious := sortedNodeScoreList[0]\n   901→\t\tsortedNodeScoreList[0] = sortedNodeScoreList[selectedIndex]\n   902→\t\tsortedNodeScoreList[selectedIndex] = previous\n   903→\t}\n   904→\n   905→\tif len(sortedNodeScoreList) > count {\n   906→\t\tsortedNodeScoreList = sortedNodeScoreList[:count]\n   907→\t}\n   908→\n   909→\treturn sortedNodeScoreList[0].Name, sortedNodeScoreList, nil\n   910→}\n   911→\n   912→// nodeScoreHeap is a heap of framework.NodePluginScores.\n   913→type nodeScoreHeap []framework.NodePluginScores\n   914→\n   915→// nodeScoreHeap implements heap.Interface.\n   916→var _ heap.Interface = &nodeScoreHeap{}\n   917→\n   918→func (h nodeScoreHeap) Len() int           { return len(h) }\n   919→func (h nodeScoreHeap) Less(i, j int) bool { return h[i].TotalScore > h[j].TotalScore }\n   920→func (h nodeScoreHeap) Swap(i, j int)      { h[i], h[j] = h[j], h[i] }\n   921→\n   922→func (h *nodeScoreHeap) Push(x interface{}) {\n   923→\t*h = append(*h, x.(framework.NodePluginScores))\n   924→}\n   925→\n   926→func (h *nodeScoreHeap) Pop() interface{} {\n   927→\told := *h\n   928→\tn := len(old)\n   929→\tx := old[n-1]\n   930→\t*h = old[0 : n-1]\n   931→\treturn x\n   932→}\n   933→\n   934→// assume signals to the cache that a pod is already in the cache, so that binding can be asynchronous.\n   935→// assume modifies `assumed`.\n   936→func (sched *Scheduler) assume(logger klog.Logger, assumed *v1.Pod, host string) error {\n   937→\t// Optimistically assume that the binding will succeed and send it to apiserver\n   938→\t// in the background.\n   939→\t// If the binding fails, scheduler will release resources allocated to assumed pod\n   940→\t// immediately.\n   941→\tassumed.Spec.NodeName = host\n   942→\n   943→\tif err := sched.Cache.AssumePod(logger, assumed); err != nil {\n   944→\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Scheduler cache AssumePod failed\")\n   945→\t\treturn err\n   946→\t}\n   947→\t// if \"assumed\" is a nominated pod, we should remove it from internal cache\n   948→\tif sched.SchedulingQueue != nil {\n   949→\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.DeleteNominatedPodIfExists(assumed)\n   950→\t}\n   951→\n   952→\treturn nil\n   953→}\n   954→\n   955→// bind binds a pod to a given node defined in a binding object.\n   956→// The precedence for binding is: (1) extenders and (2) framework plugins.\n   957→// We expect this to run asynchronously, so we handle binding metrics internally.\n   958→func (sched *Scheduler) bind(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, assumed *v1.Pod, targetNode string, state *framework.CycleState) (status *framework.Status) {\n   959→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   960→\tdefer func() {\n   961→\t\tsched.finishBinding(logger, fwk, assumed, targetNode, fwk.RunBindPlugins(ctx, state, assumed, targetNode)\n   969→}\n   970→\n   971→// TODO(#87159): Move this to a Plugin.\n   972→func (sched *Scheduler) extendersBinding(logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod, node string) (bool, error) {\n   973→\tfor _, extender := range sched.Extenders {\n   974→\t\tif !extender.IsBinder() || !extender.IsInterested(pod) {\n   975→\t\t\tcontinue\n   976→\t\t}\n \"Node\", Name: node},\n   980→\t\t})\n   981→\t\tif err != nil && extender.IsIgnorable() {\n   982→\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Skipping extender in bind as it returned error and has ignorable flag set\", \"extender\", extender, \"err\", err)\n   983→\t\t\tcontinue\n   984→\t\t}\n   985→\t\treturn true, err\n   986→\t}\n   987→\treturn false, nil\n   988→}\n   989→\n   990→func (sched *Scheduler) finishBinding(logger klog.Logger, fwk framework.Framework, assumed *v1.Pod, targetNode string, status *framework.Status) {\n   991→\tif finErr := sched.Cache.FinishBinding(logger, assumed); finErr != nil {\n   992→\t\tlogger.Error(finErr, \"Scheduler cache FinishBinding failed\")\n   993→\t}\n   994→\tif !status.IsSuccess() {\n   995→\t\tlogger.V(1).Info(\"Failed to bind pod\", \"pod\", capped to a limit\n  1004→\t// to avoid ending up with a high cardinality metric.\n  1005→\tif p.Attempts >= 15 {\n  1006→\t\treturn \"15+\"\n  1007→\t}\n  1008→\treturn strconv.Itoa(p.Attempts)\n Also, update the pod condition and nominated node name if set.\n  1013→func (sched *Scheduler) handleSchedulingFailure(ctx context.Context, fwk framework.Framework, podInfo *framework.QueuedPodInfo, status *framework.Status, nominatingInfo *framework.NominatingInfo, start time.Time) {\n  1014→\tcalledDone := false\n  1015→\tdefer func() {\n  1016→\t\tif !calledDone {\n  1017→\t\t\t// Basically, AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent calls DonePod internally.\n  1018→\t\t\t// But, AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent isn't called in some corner cases.\n  1019→\t\t\t// Here, we call DonePod explicitly to avoid leaking the pod.\n  1020→\t\t\tsched.SchedulingQueue.Done(podInfo.Pod.UID)\n  1021→\t\t}\n  1022→\t}()\n  1023→\n  1024→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n  1025→\treason := v1.PodReasonSchedulerError\n  1026→\tif status.IsRejected() {\n  1027→\t\treason = v1.PodReasonUnschedulable\n  1028→\t}\n  1029→\n  1030→\tswitch reason {\n  1031→\tcase v1.PodReasonUnschedulable:\n  1032→\t\tmetrics.PodUnschedulable(fwk.ProfileName(), metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n  1033→\tcase v1.PodReasonSchedulerError:\n  1034→\t\tmetrics.PodScheduleError(fwk.ProfileName(), metrics.SinceInSeconds(start))\n  1035→\t}\n  1036→\n  1037→\tpod := podInfo.Pod\n  1038→\terr := status.AsError()\n  1039→\terrMsg := status.Message()\n  1040→\n  1041→\tif err == ErrNoNodesAvailable {\n  1042→\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Unable to schedule pod;    67→// Constants for GVKs.\n    68→const (\n    69→\t// There are a couple of notes about how the scheduler notifies the events of Pods:\n    70→\t// - Add: add events could be triggered by either a newly created Pod or an existing Pod that is scheduled to a Node.\n    71→\t// - Delete: delete events could be triggered by:\n    72→\t//           - a Pod that is deleted\n    73→\t//           - a Pod that was assumed, but gets un-assumed due to some errors in the binding cycle.\n    74→\t//           - an existing Pod that was unscheduled but gets scheduled to a Node.\n    75→\tPod GVK = \"Pod\"\n    76→\t// A note about NodeAdd event and UpdateNodeTaint event:\n    77→\t// NodeAdd QueueingHint isn't always called because of the internal feature called preCheck.\n    78→\t// It's definitely not something expected for plugin developers,\n    79→\t// and registering UpdateNodeTaint event is the only mitigation for now.\n    80→\t// So, kube-scheduler registers UpdateNodeTaint event for plugins that has NodeAdded event, but don't have UpdateNodeTaint event.\n    81→\t// It has a bad impact for the requeuing efficiency though, a lot better than some Pods being stuck in the\n    82→\t// unschedulable pod pool.\n    83→\t// This behavior will be removed when we remove the preCheck feature.\n    84→\t// See: https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/110175\n    85→\tNode                    GVK = \"Node\"\n    86→\tPersistentVolume        GVK = \"PersistentVolume\"\n    87→\tPersistentVolumeClaim   GVK = \"PersistentVolumeClaim\"\n    88→\tCSINode admitted. 375→\treasonMsg := fmt.Sprintf(NoNodeAvailableMsg+\":\", f.NumAllNodes)\n   376→\tpreFilterMsg := f.Diagnosis.PreFilterMsg\n   377→\tif preFilterMsg != \"\" {\n   378→\t\t// PreFilter plugin returns unschedulable.\n   379→\t\t// Add the messages from PreFilter plugins to reasonMsg.\n   380→\t\treasonMsg += fmt.Sprintf(\" %v.\", preFilterMsg)\n   381→\t}\n   382→\n   383→\tif preFilterMsg == \"\" {\n   384→\t\t// the scheduling cycle went through PreFilter extension point successfully.\n   385→\t\t//\n   386→\t\t// When the prefilter plugin returns unschedulable,\n   387→\t\t// the scheduling framework inserts the same unschedulable status to all nodes in NodeToStatusMap.\n   388→\t\t// So, we shouldn't add the message from NodeToStatusMap when the PreFilter failed.\n   389→\t\t// Otherwise, we will have duplicated reasons in the error message.\n   390→\t\treasons := make(map[string]int)\n   391→\t\tfor _, status := range f.Diagnosis.NodeToStatusMap {\n   392→\t\t\tfor _, reason := range status.Reasons() {\n   393→\t\t\t\treasons[reason]++\n   394→\t\t\t}\n   395→\t\t}\n   396→\n   397→\t\tsortReasonsHistogram := func() []string {\n   398→\t\t\tvar reasonStrings []string\n   399→\t\t\tfor k, v := range reasons {\n   400→\t\t\t\treasonStrings = append(reasonStrings, fmt.Sprintf(\"%v %v\", v, k))\n   401→\t\t\t}\n   402→\t\t\tsort.Strings(reasonStrings)\n   403→\t\t\treturn reasonStrings\n   404→\t\t}\n   405→\t\tsortedFilterMsg := sortReasonsHistogram()\n   406→\t\tif len(sortedFilterMsg) != 0 {\n   407→\t\t\treasonMsg += fmt.Sprintf(\" %v.\", strings.Join(sortedFilterMsg, \", \"))\n   408→\t\t}\n   409→\t}\n   410→\n   411→\t// Add the messages from PostFilter plugins to reasonMsg.\n   412→\t// We can add this message regardless of whether the scheduling cycle fails at PreFilter or Filter\n   413→\t// since we may run PostFilter (if enabled) in both cases.\n   414→\tpostFilterMsg := f.Diagnosis.PostFilterMsg\n   415→\tif postFilterMsg != \"\" {\n   416→\t\treasonMsg += fmt.Sprintf(\" %v\", postFilterMsg)\n   417→\t}\n   418→\treturn reasonMsg\n   419→}\n   420→\n   421→func newAffinityTerm(pod *v1.Pod, term *v1.PodAffinityTerm) (*AffinityTerm, error) {\n   422→\tselector, err := metav1.LabelSelectorAsSelector(term.LabelSelector)\n   423→\tif err != nil {\n   424→\t\treturn nil, err\n   425→\t}\n   426→\n   427→\tnamespaces := getNamespacesFromPodAffinityTerm(pod, term)\n   428→\tnsSelector, err := metav1.LabelSelectorAsSelector(term.NamespaceSelector)\n   429→\tif err != nil {\n   430→\t\treturn nil, err\n   431→\t}\n   432→\n   433→\treturn &AffinityTerm{Namespaces: namespaces, Selector: selector, TopologyKey: term.TopologyKey, NamespaceSelector: nsSelector}, nil\n   434→}\n   435→\n   436→// getAffinityTerms receives a Pod and affinity terms and returns the namespaces and\n   437→// selectors of the terms.\n   438→func getAffinityTerms(pod *v1.Pod, v1Terms []v1.PodAffinityTerm) ([]AffinityTerm, error) {\n   439→\tif v1Terms == nil {\n   440→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   441→\t}\n   442→\n   443→\tvar terms []AffinityTerm\n   444→\tfor i := range v1Terms {\n   445→\t\tt, err := newAffinityTerm(pod, &v1Terms[i])\n   446→\t\tif err != nil {\n   447→\t\t\t// We get here if the label selector failed to process\n   448→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   449→\t\t}\n   450→\t\tterms = append(terms, *t)\n   451→\t}\n   452→\treturn terms, nil\n   453→}\n   454→\n   455→// getWeightedAffinityTerms returns the list of processed affinity terms.\n   456→func getWeightedAffinityTerms(pod *v1.Pod, v1Terms []v1.WeightedPodAffinityTerm) ([]WeightedAffinityTerm, error) {\n   457→\tif v1Terms == nil {\n   458→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   459→\t}\n   460→\n   461→\tvar terms []WeightedAffinityTerm\n   462→\tfor 466→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   467→\t\t}\n   468→\t\tterms = append(terms, WeightedAffinityTerm{AffinityTerm: *t, Weight: v1Terms[i].Weight})\n   469→\t}\n   470→\treturn terms, nil\n   471→}\n   472→\n   473→// NewPodInfo returns a new PodInfo.\n   474→func NewPodInfo(pod *v1.Pod) (*PodInfo, error) {\n   475→\tpInfo := &PodInfo{}\n   476→\terr := pInfo.Update(pod)\n   477→\treturn pInfo, err\n   478→}\n   479→\n   480→func getPodAffinityTerms(affinity *v1.Affinity) (terms []v1.PodAffinityTerm) {\n   481→\tif affinity != nil && affinity.PodAffinity != nil {\n   482→\t\tif returns a set of names according to the namespaces indicated in podAffinityTerm.\n   507→// If namespaces is empty it considers the given pod's namespace.\n   508→func getNamespacesFromPodAffinityTerm(pod *v1.Pod, podAffinityTerm *v1.PodAffinityTerm) sets.Set[string] {\n   509→\tnames := sets.Set[string]{}\n   510→\tif len(podAffinityTerm.Namespaces) == 0 && podAffinityTerm.NamespaceSelector == nil {\n   511→\t\tnames.Insert(pod.Namespace)\n   512→\t} else {\n   513→\t\tnames.Insert(podAffinityTerm.Namespaces...)\n   514→\t}\n   515→\treturn names\n   516→}\n   517→\n   518→// ImageStateSummary provides summarized information about the state of an image.\n   519→type ImageStateSummary struct {\n   520→\t// Size of the image\n   521→\tSize int64\n   522→\t// Used to track how many nodes have this image, it is computed from the Nodes field below\n   523→\t// during the execution of Snapshot.\n   524→\tNumNodes int\n   525→\t// A set of node names for nodes having this image present. This field is used for\n   526→\t// keeping track of the nodes during update/add/remove events.\n   527→\tNodes sets.Set[string]\n   528→}\n   529→\n   530→// Snapshot returns a copy without Nodes field of ImageStateSummary\n   531→func (iss *ImageStateSummary) Snapshot() *ImageStateSummary {\n   532→\treturn &ImageStateSummary{\n   533→\t\tSize:     iss.Size,\n   534→\t\tNumNodes: iss.Nodes.Len(),\n   535→\t}\n   536→}\n   537→\n   538→// NodeInfo is node level aggregated information.\n   539→type NodeInfo struct {\n   540→\t// Overall node information.\n   541→\tnode *v1.Node\n   542→\n   543→\t// Pods running on the node.\n   544→\tPods []*PodInfo\n   545→\n   546→\t// The subset of pods with affinity.\n   547→\tPodsWithAffinity []*PodInfo\n   548→\n   549→\t// The subset of pods with required anti-affinity.\n   550→\tPodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity []*PodInfo\n   551→\n   552→\t// Ports allocated on the node.\n   553→\tUsedPorts HostPortInfo\n   554→\n   555→\t// Total requested resources of all pods on this node. This includes assumed\n   556→\t// pods, which scheduler has sent for binding, but may not be scheduled yet.\n   557→\tRequested *Resource\n   558→\t// Total requested resources of all pods on this node with a minimum value\n   559→\t// applied to each container's CPU and memory requests. This does not reflect\n   560→\t// the actual resource requests for this node, but is used to avoid scheduling\n   561→\t// many zero-request pods onto one node.\n   562→\tNonZeroRequested *Resource\n   563→\t// We store allocatedResources (which is Node.Status.Allocatable.*) explicitly\n   564→\t// as int64, to avoid conversions and accessing map.\n   565→\tAllocatable *Resource\n   566→\n   567→\t// ImageStates holds the entry of an image if and only if this image is on the node. The entry can be used for\n   568→\t// checking an image's existence and advanced usage (e.g., image locality scheduling policy) based on the image\n   569→\t// state information.\n   570→\tImageStates map[string]*ImageStateSummary\n   571→\n   572→\t// PVCRefCounts contains a mapping of PVC names to the number of pods on the node using it.\n   573→\t// Keys are in the format \"namespace/name\".\n   574→\tPVCRefCounts map[string]int\n   575→\n   576→\t// Whenever NodeInfo changes, generation is bumped.\n   577→\t// This is used to avoid cloning it if the object didn't change.\n   578→\tGeneration int64\n   579→}\n   580→\n   581→// nextGeneration: Let's make sure history never forgets the name...\n   582→// Increments the generation number monotonically ensuring that generation numbers never collide.\n   583→// Collision of the generation numbers would be particularly problematic if a node was deleted and\n   584→// added back with the same name. See issue#63262.\n   585→func nextGeneration() int64 {\n   586→\treturn atomic.AddInt64(&generation, 1)\n   587→}\n   588→\n   589→// Resource is a collection of compute resource.\n   590→type Resource struct {\n   591→\tMilliCPU         int64\n   592→\tMemory           int64\n   593→\tEphemeralStorage int64\n   594→\t// We store allowedPodNumber (which is Node.Status.Allocatable.Pods().Value())\n   595→\t// explicitly as int, to avoid conversions and improve performance.\n   596→\tAllowedPodNumber int\n   597→\t// ScalarResources\n   598→\tScalarResources map[v1.ResourceName]int64\n   599→}\n   600→\n   601→// NewResource creates a Resource from ResourceList\n   602→func NewResource(rl v1.ResourceList) *Resource {\n   603→\tr := &Resource{}\n   604→\tr.Add(rl)\n   605→\treturn r\n   606→}\n   607→\n   608→// Add adds ResourceList into Resource.\n   609→func (r *Resource) Add(rl v1.ResourceList) {\n   610→\tif r == nil {\n   611→\t\treturn\n   612→\t}\n   613→\n   614→\tfor rName, rQuant := range rl {\n   615→\t\tswitch rName {\n   616→\t\tcase v1.ResourceCPU:\n   617→\t\t\tr.MilliCPU += rQuant.MilliValue()\n   618→\t\tcase v1.ResourceMemory:\n   619→\t\t\tr.Memory += rQuant.Value()\n   620→\t\tcase v1.ResourcePods:\n   621→\t\t\tr.AllowedPodNumber += int(rQuant.Value())\n   622→\t\tcase v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage:\n   623→\t\t\tr.EphemeralStorage += rQuant.Value()\n   624→\t\tdefault:\n   625→\t\t\tif schedutil.IsScalarResourceName(rName) {\n   626→\t\t\t\tr.AddScalar(rName, rQuant.Value())\n   627→\t\t\t}\n   628→\t\t}\n   629→\t}\n   630→}\n   631→\n   632→// Clone returns a copy of this resource.\n   633→func (r *Resource) Clone() *Resource {\n   634→\tres := &Resource{\n   635→\t\tMilliCPU:         r.MilliCPU,\n   636→\t\tMemory:           r.Memory,\n   637→\t\tAllowedPodNumber: r.AllowedPodNumber,\n   638→\t\tEphemeralStorage: r.EphemeralStorage,\n   639→\t}\n   640→\tif r.ScalarResources != nil {\n   641→\t\tres.ScalarResources = make(map[v1.ResourceName]int64, len(r.ScalarResources))\n   642→\t\tfor k, v := range r.ScalarResources {\n   643→\t\t\tres.ScalarResources[k] = v\n   644→\t\t}\n   645→\t}\n   646→\treturn res\n   647→}\n   648→\n   649→// AddScalar adds a resource by a scalar value of this resource.\n   650→func (r *Resource) AddScalar(name v1.ResourceName, quantity int64) {\n   651→\tr.SetScalar(name, r.ScalarResources[name]+quantity)\n   652→}\n   653→\n   654→// SetScalar sets a resource by a scalar value of this resource.\n   655→func (r *Resource) SetScalar(name v1.ResourceName, quantity int64) {\n   656→\t// Lazily allocate scalar resource map.\n   657→\tif r.ScalarResources == nil {\n   658→\t\tr.ScalarResources = map[v1.ResourceName]int64{}\n   659→\t}\n   660→\tr.ScalarResources[name] = quantity\n   661→}\n   662→\n   663→// SetMaxResource compares with ResourceList and takes max value for each Resource.\n   664→func (r *Resource) SetMaxResource(rl v1.ResourceList) {\n   665→\tif r == nil {\n   666→\t\treturn\n   667→\t}\n   668→\n   669→\tfor rName, rQuantity := range rl {\n   670→\t\tswitch rName {\n   671→\t\tcase v1.ResourceMemory:\n   672→\t\t\tr.Memory = max(r.Memory, rQuantity.Value())\n   673→\t\tcase v1.ResourceCPU:\n   674→\t\t\tr.MilliCPU = max(r.MilliCPU, rQuantity.MilliValue())\n   675→\t\tcase v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage:\n   676→\t\t\tr.EphemeralStorage = max(r.EphemeralStorage, rQuantity.Value())\n   677→\t\tdefault:\n   678→\t\t\tif schedutil.IsScalarResourceName(rName) {\n   679→\t\t\t\tr.SetScalar(rName, max(r.ScalarResources[rName], rQuantity.Value()))\n   680→\t\t\t}\n   681→\t\t}\n   682→\t}\n   683→}\n   684→\n   685→// NewNodeInfo returns a ready to use empty NodeInfo object.\n   686→// If any pods are given in arguments, their information will be aggregated in\n   687→// the returned object.\n   688→func NewNodeInfo(pods ...*v1.Pod) *NodeInfo {\n   689→\tni := &NodeInfo{\n   690→\t\tRequested:        &Resource{},\n   691→\t\tNonZeroRequested: &Resource{},\n   692→\t\tAllocatable:      &Resource{},\n   693→\t\tGeneration:       nextGeneration(),\n   694→\t\tUsedPorts:        make(HostPortInfo),\n   695→\t\tImageStates:      make(map[string]*ImageStateSummary),\n   696→\t\tPVCRefCounts:     make(map[string]int),\n   697→\t}\n   698→\tfor _, pod := range pods {\n   699→\t\tni.AddPod(pod)\n   700→\t}\n   701→\treturn ni\n   702→}\n   703→\n   704→// Node returns overall information about this node.\n   705→func (n *NodeInfo) Node() *v1.Node {\n   706→\tif n == nil {\n   707→\t\treturn nil\n   708→\t}\n   709→\treturn n.node\n   710→}\n   711→\n   712→// Snapshot returns a copy of this node, Except that ImageStates is copied without the Nodes field.\n   713→func (n *NodeInfo) Snapshot() *NodeInfo {\n   714→\tclone := &NodeInfo{\n   715→\t\tnode:             n.node,\n   716→\t\tRequested:        n.Requested.Clone(),\n   717→\t\tNonZeroRequested: n.NonZeroRequested.Clone(),\n   718→\t\tAllocatable:      n.Allocatable.Clone(),\n   719→\t\tUsedPorts:        make(HostPortInfo),\n   720→\t\tImageStates:      make(map[string]*ImageStateSummary),\n   721→\t\tPVCRefCounts:     make(map[string]int),\n   722→\t\tGeneration:       n.Generation,\n   723→\t}\n   724→\tif len(n.Pods) > 0 {\n   725→\t\tclone.Pods = append([]*PodInfo(nil), n.Pods...)\n   726→\t}\n   727→\tif len(n.UsedPorts) > 0 {\n   728→\t\t// HostPortInfo is a map-in-map struct\n   729→\t\t// make sure it's deep copied\n   730→\t\tfor ip, portMap := range n.UsedPorts {\n   731→\t\t\tclone.UsedPorts[ip] = make(map[ProtocolPort]struct{})\n   732→\t\t\tfor protocolPort, v := range portMap {\n   733→\t\t\t\tclone.UsedPorts[ip][protocolPort] = v\n   734→\t\t\t}\n   735→\t\t}\n   736→\t}\n   737→\tif len(n.PodsWithAffinity) > 0 {\n   738→\t\tclone.PodsWithAffinity = append([]*PodInfo(nil), n.PodsWithAffinity...)\n   739→\t}\n   740→\tif len(n.PodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity) > 0 {\n   741→\t\tclone.PodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity = append([]*PodInfo(nil), n.PodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity...)\n   742→\t}\n   743→\tif len(n.ImageStates) > 0 {\n   744→\t\tstate := make(map[string]*ImageStateSummary, len(n.ImageStates))\n   745→\t\tfor imageName, imageState := range n.ImageStates {\n   746→\t\t\tstate[imageName] = imageState.Snapshot()\n   747→\t\t}\n   748→\t\tclone.ImageStates = state\n   749→\t}\n   750→\tfor key, value := range n.PVCRefCounts {\n   751→\t\tclone.PVCRefCounts[key] = value\n   752→\t}\n   753→\treturn clone\n   754→}\n   755→\n   756→// String returns representation of human readable format of this NodeInfo.\n   757→func (n *NodeInfo) String() string {\n   758→\tpodKeys := make([]string, len(n.Pods))\n   759→\tfor i, p := range n.Pods {\n   760→\t\tpodKeys[i] = p.Pod.Name\n   761→\t}\n   762→\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"&NodeInfo{Pods:%v, RequestedResource:%#v, NonZeroRequest: %#v, UsedPort: %#v, AllocatableResource:%#v}\",\n   763→\t\tpodKeys, n.Requested, n.NonZeroRequested, n.UsedPorts, n.Allocatable)\n   764→}\n   765→\n   766→// AddPodInfo adds pod information to this NodeInfo.\n   767→// Consider using this instead of AddPod if a PodInfo is already computed.\n   768→func (n *NodeInfo) AddPodInfo(podInfo *PodInfo) {\n   769→\tn.Pods = append(n.Pods, podInfo)\n   770→\tif podWithAffinity(podInfo.Pod) {\n   771→\t\tn.PodsWithAffinity = append(n.PodsWithAffinity, podInfo)\n   772→\t}\n   773→\tif podWithRequiredAntiAffinity(podInfo.Pod) {\n   774→\t\tn.PodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity = append(n.PodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity, podInfo)\n   775→\t}\n   776→\tn.update(podInfo.Pod, 1)\n   777→}\n   778→\n   779→// AddPod is a wrapper around AddPodInfo.\n   780→func (n *NodeInfo) AddPod(pod *v1.Pod) {\n   781→\t// ignore this err since apiserver doesn't properly validate affinity terms\n   782→\t// and we can't fix the validation for backwards compatibility.\n   783→\tpodInfo, _ := NewPodInfo(pod)\n   784→\tn.AddPodInfo(podInfo)\n   785→}\n   786→\n   787→func podWithAffinity(p *v1.Pod) bool {\n   788→\taffinity := p.Spec.Affinity\n   789→\treturn affinity != nil && (affinity.PodAffinity != nil || affinity.PodAntiAffinity != nil)\n   790→}\n   791→\n   792→func podWithRequiredAntiAffinity(p *v1.Pod) bool {\n   793→\taffinity := p.Spec.Affinity\n   794→\treturn affinity != nil && affinity.PodAntiAffinity != nil &&\n   795→\t\tlen(affinity.PodAntiAffinity.RequiredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution) != 0\n   796→}\n   797→\n   798→func removeFromSlice(logger klog.Logger, s []*PodInfo, k string) ([]*PodInfo, bool) {\n   799→\tvar removed bool\n   800→\tfor i := range s {\n   801→\t\ttmpKey, err := GetPodKey(s[i].Pod)\n   802→\t\tif err != nil {\n   803→\t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Cannot get pod key\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(s[i].Pod))\n   804→\t\t\tcontinue\n   805→\t\t}\n   806→\t\tif k == tmpKey {\n   807→\t\t\t// delete the element\n   808→\t\t\ts[i] = s[len(s)-1]\n   809→\t\t\ts = s[:len(s)-1]\n   810→\t\t\tremoved = true\n   811→\t\t\tbreak\n   812→\t\t}\n   813→\t}\n   814→\t// resets the slices to nil so that we can do DeepEqual in unit tests.\n   815→\tif len(s) == 0 {\n   816→\t\treturn nil, removed\n   817→\t}\n   818→\treturn s, removed\n   819→}\n   820→\n   821→// RemovePod subtracts pod information from this NodeInfo.\n   822→func (n *NodeInfo) RemovePod(logger klog.Logger, pod *v1.Pod) error {\n   823→\tk, err := GetPodKey(pod)\n   824→\tif err != nil {\n   825→\t\treturn err\n   826→\t}\n   827→\tif podWithAffinity(pod) {\n   828→\t\tn.PodsWithAffinity, _ = removeFromSlice(logger, n.PodsWithAffinity, k)\n   829→\t}\n   830→\tif podWithRequiredAntiAffinity(pod) {\n   831→\t\tn.PodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity, _ = removeFromSlice(logger, n.PodsWithRequiredAntiAffinity, k)\n   832→\t}\n   833→\n   834→\tvar removed bool\n   835→\tif n.Pods, removed = removeFromSlice(logger, n.Pods, k); removed {\n   836→\t\tn.update(pod, -1)\n   837→\t\treturn nil\n   838→\t}\n   839→\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"no corresponding pod %s in pods of node %s\", pod.Name, n.node.Name)\n   840→}\n   841→\n   842→// update node info based on the pod and sign.\n   843→// The sign will be set to `+1` when AddPod and to `-1` when RemovePod.\n   844→func (n *NodeInfo) update(pod *v1.Pod, sign int64) {\n   845→\tres, non0CPU, non0Mem := calculateResource(pod)\n   846→\tn.Requested.MilliCPU += sign * res.MilliCPU\n   847→\tn.Requested.Memory += sign * res.Memory\n   848→\tn.Requested.EphemeralStorage += sign * res.EphemeralStorage\n   849→\tif n.Requested.ScalarResources == nil && len(res.ScalarResources) > 0 {\n   850→\t\tn.Requested.ScalarResources = map[v1.ResourceName]int64{}\n   851→\t}\n   852→\tfor rName, rQuant := range res.ScalarResources {\n   853→\t\tn.Requested.ScalarResources[rName] += sign * rQuant\n   854→\t}\n   855→\tn.NonZeroRequested.MilliCPU += sign * non0CPU\n   856→\tn.NonZeroRequested.Memory += sign * non0Mem\n   857→\n   858→\t// Consume ports when pod added or release ports when pod removed.\n   859→\tn.updateUsedPorts(pod, sign > 0)\n   860→\tn.updatePVCRefCounts(pod, sign > 0)\n   861→\n   862→\tn.Generation = nextGeneration()\n   863→}\n   864→\n   865→func calculateResource(pod *v1.Pod) (Resource, int64, int64) {\n   866→\tvar non0InitCPU, non0InitMem int64\n   867→\tvar non0CPU, non0Mem int64\n   868→\trequests := resourcehelper.PodRequests(pod, resourcehelper.PodResourcesOptions{\n   869→\t\tInPlacePodVerticalScalingEnabled: utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.InPlacePodVerticalScaling),\n   870→\t\tContainerFn: func(requests v1.ResourceList, containerType podutil.ContainerType) {\n   871→\t\t\tnon0CPUReq, non0MemReq := schedutil.GetNonzeroRequests(&requests)\n   872→\t\t\tswitch containerType {\n   873→\t\t\tcase podutil.Containers:\n   874→\t\t\t\tnon0CPU += non0CPUReq\n   875→\t\t\t\tnon0Mem += non0MemReq\n   876→\t\t\tcase podutil.InitContainers:\n   877→\t\t\t\tnon0InitCPU = max(non0InitCPU, non0CPUReq)\n   878→\t\t\t\tnon0InitMem = max(non0InitMem, non0MemReq)\n   879→\t\t\t}\n can uniquely represent a particular API resource.\ntype GVK string\n\n// Constants for GVKs.\nconst (\n\t// There are a couple of notes about how the scheduler notifies the events of Pods:\n\t// - Add: add events could be triggered by either a newly created Pod or an existing Pod that is scheduled to a Node.\n\t// - Delete: delete events could be triggered by:\n\t//           - a Pod that is deleted\n\t//           - a Pod that was assumed, but gets un-assumed due to some errors in the binding cycle.\n\t//           - an existing Pod that was unscheduled but gets scheduled to a Node.\n\tPod GVK = \"Pod\"\n\t// A note about NodeAdd event and UpdateNodeTaint event:\n\t// NodeAdd QueueingHint isn't always called because of the internal feature called preCheck.\n\t// It's definitely not something expected for plugin developers,\n\t// and registering UpdateNodeTaint event is the only mitigation for now.\n\t// So, kube-scheduler registers UpdateNodeTaint event for plugins that has NodeAdded event, but don't have UpdateNodeTaint event.\n\t// It has a bad impact for the requeuing efficiency though, a lot better than some Pods being stuck in the\n\t// unschedulable pod pool.\n\t// This behavior will be removed when we remove the preCheck feature.\n\t// See: https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/110175\n\tNode                    GVK = \"ResourceClass\"\n\tResourceClaimParameters GVK = \"ResourceClaimParameters\"\n\tResourceClassParameters GVK = \"ResourceClassParameters\"\n\n\t// WildCard is a special GVK to match all
